##  100037000	ORANJE				1008000	
100037000={# WILLEM IV Karel Hendrik Friso, Pr of Nassau-Dietz, Pr of Orange, confirmed as Hereditary Stattholder of the United Provinces (the Netherlands) 4 May 1747 (Leeuwarden 1 Sep 1711-The Hague 22 Oct 1751); m.St.James's Palace 25 Mar 1734 Anne, Pss Royal of Great Britain, Ireland and Hannover, etc (Hannover 2 Nov 1709-The Hague 12 Jan 1759)
	name=Willem
	dynasty=1008000
	religion=lutheran culture=dutch
	1711.09.01={birth=yes}
	1734.03.25={add_spouse=100105206}	# Anne Royal of Great Britain Ireland and Hannover etc
	1751.10.22={death=yes}
}
	100037002={# 1a) Karolina (Leeuwarden 28 Feb 1743-Kirchheimbolanden 6 May 1787); m.The Hague 5 Mar 1760 Karl Christian Fst von Nassau-Weilburg (Weilburg 16 Jan 1735-Münster-Dreyssen, nr Kirchheim 28 Nov 1788); Note: I originally followed other sources and showed her name to be Wilhelmina Karolina, but I received the following information from Bearn Bilker: "She didn't have the name Wilhelmina, in the 19th centruy sources added probably this name for national reasons . But in all real original sources, even her testament, she only wears the name CAROLINA. The same of her little sister, Anna (1746-1746) born and died in Leeuwarden. She didn't have the 	name Marie. Of course we have the christening acts here in Leeuwarden."
